 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql

  ?song wdt:P31 wd:Q7366;      # instance of a song

    ?album wdt:P31 wd:Q482994; # instance of album
           wdt:P175 wd:Q238819; # performed by Jay Chou
           wdt:P361 ?song.      # includes song
  }
  FILTER(!BOUND(?album))       # song not included in any of Jay Chou's albums
}
```

 Generated sparql query:

```sparql
LIMIT 1
OFFSET 1
```

PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> SELECT ?result WHERE {wd:Q30 wdt:P1813 ?name BIND(lang(?name) AS ?result)} ORDER BY ASC(strlen(?name)) LIMIT 1
 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql
SELECT ?language ?shortNameLength
WHERE {
  wd:Q30 wdt:P1813 ?shortName.
  BIND(STRLEN(?shortName) AS ?shortNameLength).
  ?shortName rdfs:label ?shortNameLabel.
  FILTER(LANG(?shortNameLabel) = LANG(?shortName)).
  BIND(LANG(?shortName) AS ?language)
}
ORDER BY ASC(?shortNameLength)
LIMIT 1
```

PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> ASK {{SELECT (COUNT (DISTINCT ?ac) AS ?acc) (COUNT (DISTINCT ?ec) AS ?ecc) WHERE {?ec p:P31/ps:P31 wd:Q6256; wdt:P30 wd:Q46. ?ac p:P31/ps:P31 wd:Q6256; wdt:P30 wd:Q48.}}FILTER(?ecc > ?acc)}

```sparql
  {
    ?countryAsia wdt:P31 wd:Q6256; wdt:P30 wd:Q48.
  }
}
HAVING (?EuropeCount > ?AsiaCount)
```

 Natural language question: Which archipelago has more islands: the Galápagos Islands or the Hawaiian Islands ?

 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql
SELECT ?archipelagoLabel (COUNT(?island) AS ?islandCount)
WHERE {
  VALUES ?archipelago { wd:Q38095 wd:Q23442 }
  ?archipelago wdt:P527 ?island.
  ?island wdt:P31/wdt:P279* wd:Q192626.
  SERVICE wikibase:label { bd:serviceParam wikibase:language "[AUTO_LANGUAGE],en". }
}
GROUP BY ?archipelagoLabel
ORDER BY DESC(?islandCount)
LIMIT 1
```

 Natural language question: Did Germany have a population growth of at least 1% since 2010?
 Correct SPARQL query: 
PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> ASK {wd:Q183 p:P1082 ?ps10, ?psNew. ?ps10 pq:P585 ?t10; ps:P1082 ?p10. ?psNew pq:P585 ?tNew; ps:P1082 ?pNew BIND(((?pNew - ?p10) / ?p10) AS ?diff) FILTER((YEAR(?t10) = 2010) && NOT EXISTS{wd:Q183 p:P1082/pq:P585 ?tt FILTER(?tt > ?tNew)} && ?diff >= 0.01)}
 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql
ASK {
  wd:Q183 p:P1082 [
    ps:P1082 ?population2010;
    pq:P585 ?date2010
  ], [
    ps:P1082 ?populationRecent;
    pq:P585 ?dateRecent
  ].

  FILTER(YEAR(?date2010) = 2010)
  FILTER(YEAR(?dateRecent) > 2010)
  
  BIND(((?populationRecent - ?population2010) / ?population2010 * 100) AS ?growthPercentage)
  FILTER(?growthPercentage >= 1)
}
```

 Correct SPARQL query: 
PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> SELECT DISTINCT ?result WHERE {{SELECT (COUNT (DISTINCT ?lanS) AS ?lanSCount) WHERE {wd:Q258 wdt:P37 ?lanS}} {SELECT (COUNT (DISTINCT ?lanE) AS ?lanECount) WHERE {wd:Q115 wdt:P37 ?lanE}} BIND(IF(?lanSCount > ?lanECount, wd:Q258, wd:Q115) AS ?result)}
 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql

  {
    BIND(wd:Q258 AS ?country)
    ?country wdt:P37 ?languages.
    BIND("South Africa" AS ?countryName)
  } UNION {
    BIND(wd:Q115 AS ?country)
    ?country wdt:P37 ?languages.
    BIND("Ethiopia" AS ?countryName)
  }
  BIND(COUNT(?languages) AS ?count)
} GROUP BY ?country ?countryName ORDER BY DESC(?count) LIMIT 1
```

 Correct SPARQL query:

QueryNumber: 344
 Natural language question: Who was an actor in more movies, Daniel Day Lewis or Paul Dano ?
 Correct SPARQL query: 
PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> SELECT DISTINCT ?result WHERE {{SELECT (COUNT (DISTINCT ?film) AS ?ddl) WHERE {?film wdt:P161 wd:Q166389; wdt:P31 wd:Q11424}} {SELECT (COUNT (DISTINCT ?film) AS ?pd) WHERE {?film wdt:P161 wd:Q343616; wdt:P31 wd:Q11424}} BIND(IF((?ddl > ?pd), wd:Q166389, wd:Q343616) AS ?result)}
 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql
SELECT ?actor (COUNT(?movie) AS ?movieCount) WHERE {
  VALUES ?actor { wd:Q343616 wd:Q166389 }
  ?movie wdt:P161 ?actor .
  ?movie wdt:P31 wd:Q11424 .
} 
GROUP BY ?actor
ORDER BY DESC(?movieCount)
LIMIT 1
```
 Recall: 1.0
 Accuracy: 1
 Precision: 1.0
 Query error LLM: False
 Query error dataset: False
